# 🔐 SAP T-Code Authorization Objects Reference
> **Source:** USOBT_C table (SU24 data) — exported directly from SAP S/4HANA system
> **Date:** March 2026
> **Note:** Data based on actual system — not documentation or manual knowledge!

---

## 📑 Structure
```
PART 1 — Standard SAP (SAP GUI)
  ├── BASIS
  ├── FI (Financial Accounting)
  ├── CO (Controlling)
  ├── MM (Materials Management)
  ├── SD (Sales & Distribution)
  ├── HR (Human Resources)
  ├── PP (Production Planning)
  ├── PM (Plant Maintenance)
  ├── QM (Quality Management)
  └── PS (Project System)

PART 2 — Fiori T-codes
  └── /UI2/, /UI5/, /UIF/ namespace

PART 3 — Partner/Namespace T-codes
  └── All /NAMESPACE/ T-codes
```

---

# PART 1 — Standard SAP (SAP GUI)
